Remove unused dependencies

These dependencies are in your Cargo.toml but no references were found in your source code. You can remove them by deleting the line from [dependencies]. If a dependency has 0 deps saved, it's also pulled in transitively by something else, so removing it only cleans up your manifest without shrinking the build.

Disable unnecessary features

These dependencies are already optional in their upstream crate, but are being pulled in by a feature you have enabled (often the default features). You can reduce your dependency count by changing the feature flags in your Cargo.toml — for example, adding default-features = false and listing only the features you actually need.

  • (-22 deps) ravif is already optional in image (already optional) — enabled by feature(s) avif show diff
    # Cargo.toml
    # feature(s) "avif" of image pull in ravif
    - image = { version = "...", features = ["avif"] }
    + image = { version = "..." } # without "avif"
  • (-4 deps) hf-hub is already optional in tokenizers (already optional) — enabled by feature(s) hf-hub, http show diff
    # Cargo.toml
    # feature(s) "hf-hub", "http" of tokenizers pull in hf-hub
    - tokenizers = { version = "...", features = ["hf-hub", "http"] }
    + tokenizers = { version = "..." } # without "hf-hub", "http"
  • (-4 deps) exr is already optional in image (already optional) — default feature(s) default-formats, exr pull it in; disable defaults and keep only what you need show diff
    # Cargo.toml
    # default feature(s) "default-formats", "exr" of image pull in exr
    - image = "..."
    + image = { version = "...", default-features = false, features = ["rayon"] }
  • (-3 deps) pbkdf2 is already optional in zip (already optional) — default feature(s) aes-crypto pull it in; disable defaults and keep only what you need show diff
    # Cargo.toml
    # default feature(s) "aes-crypto" of zip pull in pbkdf2
    - zip = "..."
    + zip = { version = "...", default-features = false, features = ["bzip2", "deflate64", "deflate", "lzma", "ppmd", "time", "zstd", "xz"] }

Make dependencies optional

These dependencies are always compiled but could be made optional by adding optional = true in your Cargo.toml and defining a feature flag in [features]. This lets downstream users (or your own binary crate) opt out of them when they're not needed.

  • (-56 deps) Make polars optional in modern-lstm — put it behind a Cargo feature flag show diff
    # Cargo.toml — [dependencies]
    - polars = "0.53.0"
    + polars = { version = "0.53.0", optional = true }
    # add a feature flag so users can opt in to this dependency:
    # Cargo.toml — [features]
    + use-polars = ["dep:polars"] # pick a name that makes sense for your crate
  • (-9 deps) Make opentelemetry-otlp optional in dop_timer — put it behind a Cargo feature flag show diff
